 Nutrition societies across the globe are trying to adopt this practice from ancient cultures

 Health is not a size, it's a state
 a state of harmony, in the mind and body and between people and planet

 notebandi ko lekar sarkaar lagaataar kai raste talashne kii koshish rahi he, jisamen ek tha petrol pump se bhi 2000 tak rupee nikaalnaa
 But it is not easy to get money from petrol pumps, in fact, President of All India Petrol Pump Dealers Association Ajay Bansal has said that many petrol pumps are still not equipped with machines
 unhone daawa kiya 3 se 4 din main saare petrol pump par mashin lag jaaengi
 But the big problem is with the cash, because the banks are not getting cash from them
 kuch jagahon par bainko se kareeb 1 lakh tak hi mil paa rahe hai, jisase wo zyada se zyada 50 logon ko hi de sakate hai
 Regarding which the Petrol Pump Association has demanded Rs 5 lakh from the government and banks, but has not received any reply so far
 yani agar mashin lag bhi jaaenge to bhi logo ko paisa nahi de paaenge
 At the same time, ICICI and HDFC banks have also been asked to install machines
 esbiai sirf 1 lakh rupee hi petrol panpon ke liye de rahaa he
